saaqcio sazogadoeba gaerTianebuli eleqtrosistema `saqrusener-


gom~ 1999 wlis 4 agvistos saxelmwifo kompania `eleqtrogadacemis~


(SemdgomSi - ss `eleqtrogadacema) winaaRmdeg sarCeliT mimarTa


Tbilisis saolqo sasamarTlos.


mosarCelem miuTiTa, rom mxareebs Soris 1999 wels dadebuli


xelSekrulebiT mopasuxe saxelmwifo kompania `eleqtrogadacema~


valdebuli iyo mieRo ss `ei-i-es TelasTan~ gaformebuli xel-


SekrulebiT ss `ei-i-es TelasisaTvis~ miwodebuli eleqtroenergiis


momsaxurebisaTvis gankuTvnili mTliani Tanxa, saidanac mosarCeles


anu ss gaerTianebul energosistema `saqrusenergos~ Cauricxavda ele-


qtro-gatarebisaTvis kuTvnil Tanxas 1999 wlis 1 ianvridan 1999 wlis 1


maisis CaTvliT. am periodis gadauxdelma Tanxam Seadgina 1143561


lari. mosarCelem moiTxova am Tanxis mopasuxisaTvis gadasaxdelad


dakisreba.


1999 wlis 28 seqtembris dauswrebeli gadawyvetilebiT sarCeli


dakmayofilda nawilobriv da ss `eleqtrogadacemas~ gadasaxdelad


daekisra 877061 lari da 14 TeTri.


1999 wlis 17 oqtombers ss `eleqtrogadacemam~ saCivriT mimarTa


Tbilisis saolqo sasamarTlos da moiTxova am saqmeze saolqo


sasamarTlos mier miRebuli dauswrebeli gadawyvetilebis gauqmeba im


motiviT, rom sasamarTlo sxdomaze mopasuxis warmomadgenlis


gamoucxadebloba gamowveuli iyo misi uecari avadmyofobiT, rac


sasamarTlos sapatiod unda CaeTvala.


1999 wlis 22 oqtombers Tbilisis saolqo sasamarTlos samoqalaqo da


samewarmeo saqmeTa kolegiam ganixila zemoT miTiTebuli saCivari,


magram ar daakmayofila igi da ucvlelad datova am saqmeze saolqo


1193


sasamarTlos mier miRebuli dauswrebeli gadawyvetileba im safuZvliT,


rom saCivris avtors ss `eleqtrogadacemis~ warmomadgenels avadmyofo-


bis damadasturebeli sabuTi sasamarTlo procesze ar warudgenia.


saqarTvelos uzenaesma sasamarTlom 2000 wlis 19 ivlisis


ganCinebiT gaauqma am saqmeze saolqo sasamarTlos mier 1999 wlis 22


oqtombers miRebuli ganCineba da saqme xelaxali ganxilvisaTvis


daubruna saolqo sasamarTlos.


2000 wlis 19 oqtombers mopasuxis TxovniT saqmeSi mesame pirad,


damoukidebeli sasarCelo moTxovnis gareSe, Cabmul iqna `saqenergo


2000~, xolo imave dRis sxdomaze adgilze TaTbiriT saolqo sasa-


marTlom gaauqma Tbilisis saolqo sasamarTlos mier am saqmeze 1999


wlis 28 seqtembers miRebuli dauswrebeli gadawyvetileba da Seudga


saqmis arsebiTad ganxilvas.


2001 wlis 12 Tebervlis gadawyvetilebiT sarCeli dakmayofilda.


mopasuxe ss `eleqtrogadacemas~ mosarCele ss gaerTianebuli ener-


getikuli sistema `saqrusenergos~ sasargeblod gadasaxdelad daek-


isra 877061,14 lari da ganesazRvra misi gadaxdis wesi, masve gadasaxde-


lad daekisra saxelmwifo baJis saxiT gadaxdili Tanxis 5000 laris -


`saqrusenergos~ sasargeblod gadaxda.


saolqo sasamarTlom dadgenilad miiCnia Semdegi faqtobrivi gare-


moebebi:


1999 wels ss gaerTianebul energetikul sistema `saqrusenergosa~


da ss `eleqtrogadacemas~ Soris daido xelSekruleba, romliTac


mosarCeles mopasuxisaTvis unda miewodebina eleqtroenergia, romel-


ic Tavis mxriv aanazRaurebda mis Rirebulebas, `ei-i-es TelasisaTvis~


miwodebuli eleqtroenergiis safasuridan am ukanasknelis mier


Tanxebis Camoricxvis Semdeg.


1999 wlis 17 ivniss mxareTa Soris Sedga Sedarebis aqti, romliTac


1999 wlis 1 ivnisis mdgomareobiT ss `eleqtrogadacemis~ davalianeba


ganisazRvra 1143561,14 lariT.


saolqo sasamarTlom dadgenilad miiCnia, rom 1999 wlis ivnissa da


agvistoSi mopasuxem ss gaerTianebul energetikul sistema `saqrusen-


ergos~ gadauxada 266500 lari.


saolqo sasamarTlom, aseve, dadgenilad miiCnia, rom mxareebs Soris


dadebuli xelSekruleba iyo pirobiTi garigeba. am garigebis mixedviT


ss `eleqtrogadacemas~ mosarCelis winaSe miwodebuli eleqtroenergi-


is safasuris gadaxdis valdebuleba warmoeSoboda `ei-i-es Telasis~


mier ss `eleqtrogadacemisaTvis~ momsaxurebis mTliani safasuris

mimarTa saqarTvelos uzenaes sasamarTlos. kasatorma moiTxova am


saqmeze saolqo sasamarTlos mier miRebuli gadawyvetilebis gauqmeba

gadawyvetileba iuridiulad dausabuTebelia. gadawyvetilebis


dausabuTebloba ki imaSi gamoixateba, rom mxareebs Soris gaformebuli


xelSekruleba iyo pirobiTi xelSekruleba, romlis 2.3 punqti

iyvnen gaeTvaliswinebinaT `ei-i-es Telasis~ mier wamoyenebuli yvela

mier nakisri valdebulebis Seusruleblobasac da urTierTangariS-


sworebis dros valdebulni iyvnen gaeTvaliswinebinaT aRniSnuli.

363 brZanebulebiT dadgenili kursis


mixedviT ekuTvnis 60 lari. saapelacio sasamarTlos palatis mier


damtkicebulad aris cnobili, rom l. j-Svili bankisagan moiTxovda


valdebulebis Sesrulebas. es garemoeba samoqalaqo saproceso kodeq-


sis 407-e muxlis II nawilis Tanaxmad, savaldebuloa sasamarTlosaTvis.


kasatori ver miuTiTebs raime mtkicebulebaze, romelic saapelacio


sasamarTlos mier ar iqna Seswavlili da gamokvleuli da romelic


gamoricxavda dadgenil garemoebebs.


sakasacio sasamarTlo inflaciis gaTvaliswinebiT Tanxis


gaangariSebas ver daeTanxmeba da Tvlis, rom am nawilSi sasamarTlos


gadawyvetileba dausabuTebelia, ris gamoc igi unda gauqmdes da


miRebul iqnes axali gadawyvetileba.


sakasacio sasamarTlos miaCnia, rom fuladi valdebuleba unda


sruldebodes nominalizmis principiT, rac niSnavs, rom movale valde-


bulia, vali daabrunos fuladi niSnebis imave raodenobiT, romelic


Seesabameba valdebulebis warmoSobis dros. dadgenilia, rom ss


`agromrewvbanks~ valdebuleba unda Seesrulebina 1993 wlis 28 seqtem-


bers, roca erovnuli bankidan miiRo Tanxmoba Tanxis konvertaciaze.


valdebulebis warmoSobis dros, e.i. 1993 wlis 28 seqtembers, movales


l. j-SvilisaTvis unda daebrunebina 60 milioni kuponi, gamoxatuli


aSS dolarebSi, rac im periodisaTvis Seadgenda 4 980 aSS dolars. aSS


dolaris mimarT inflaciur movlenebs adgili ara hqonia.


aRniSnulidan gamomdinare, mopasuxe valdebulia daabrunos igive


raodenoba, rac valdebulebis warmoSobis dros unda daebrunebina,


e.i. 4980 aSS dolari.


fuladi valdebulebis vadis gadacilebisas wamoiWreba procentisa


da zianis anazRaurebis sakiTxi. zianis anazRaureba mosarCeles ar


1200


mouTxovia, xolo rac Seexeba procents, igi am SemTxvevaSi warmoadgens


sxvisi fuladi saxsrebis ukanono sargeblobis Sedegs, romlis ode-


nobac ganisazRvreba kanoniT an xelSekrulebiT.


samoqalaqo samarTlis kodeqsis (1964 w.) 225-e muxlis Tanaxmad,


movalem, romelmac gadaacila fuladi valdebulebis Sesrulebis


vadas, unda gadaixados gadacilebuli drois sami procenti, Tu


kanoniT an xelSekrulebiT ar aris dadgenili procentis sxva raode-


noba. 1993 wlis 28 seqtembridan gasulia 7 weli da 9 Tve. 4 980 aSS


dolaris wliuri sami procenti Seadgens 149,4 aSS dolars, 7 wlis da 9

mimarT da moiTxova damxmare saTavsis mikuTvneba. sarCelis safuZvlad


miuTiTebda, rom mopasuxem daikava misi kuTvnili sakuWnao, romliTac


sargeblobda 1976 wlidan.


mopasuxem sarCeli ar cno da ganmarta, rom 1999 wels SeiZina


oroTaxiani bina sardafTan erTad. sardafis teritoriaze


ganTavsebuli iyo sadavo saTavsi, romliTac aravin sargeblobda. binis


SeZenis Semdeg Caatara saremonti samuSaoebi, gaamagra sardafis


saZirkveli da kedlebi, ra drosac gaauqma sadavo sakuWnao.


q. Tbilisis krwanisi-mTawmindis raionuli sasamarTlos 2000 wlis

ofilebaze.

mxareebi cxovroben TbilisSi, ... mdebare mravalbinian saxlSi, sadac

kv.m sakuTrebis uflebiT ekuTvnis mosarCeles, xolo imave ezoSi


oroTaxiani sacxovrebeli bina, farTiT 32kv.m., 4,5kv.m. samzareuloTi


da 15kv.m. sardafiT ekuTvnis mopasuxes, 1999 wels k. p-ovTan dadebuli


nasyidobis xelSekrulebis safuZvelze. sadavo farTi, zomiT 1kv.m.,


warmoadgens yofil saerTo sargeblobis sapirfareSos, romelic 70-ian


wlebSi mobinadreebma gaauqmes sveli wertilebisa da kanalizaciis


individualurad mowyobasTan dakaSirebiT. sadavo saTavsi


aRiarebulia rogorc unebarTvo, igi iyo usargeblod mitovebuli da


ar warmoadgenda aravis sakuTrebas. saTavsSi moTavsebuli iyo


mosarCele n. T-Svilis kuTvnili, saxmarad uvargisi Zveli nivTebi. 1999


wels mopasuxem Caatara saremonto samuSaoebi mis kuTvnil binasa da


sardafSi, ra drosac saTavsidan gatanil iqna n. T-Svilis Zveli, sax-


marad uvargisi nivTebi, kapitalurad SekeTda avariuli sardafis


saZirkveli da ngrevis piras misuli kedlebi. sadavo farTi aris mcire


zomis (1kv.m.), emijneba mopasuxis sakuTrebaSi arsebul sardafs,


damoukidebeli Sesasvleli ara aqvs da misi sargebloba SeiZleba


mxolod mopasuxis kuTvnili farTis gavliT. mopasuxes sxva saTavsi,


garda 15kv.m. sardafisa, ar gaaCnia,  xolo mosarCeles sakuTrebaSi aqvs


67,40kv.m damxmare farTi. sasamarTlom gamoiyena samoqalaqo kodeqsis

mtkicebuleba, romliTac dadgindeboda rom g. c-Svili iyo kooperativ


`fanaskertelis~ mepaie, rogorc TviTon uTiTebs da mSeneblobaze

damadasturebeli mtkicebulebac, rom g. c-Svilsa da kooperativ


`fanaskertels~ Soris arsebobda werilobiTi Tu zepiri garigeba.

sakuTrebis damadasturebeli mowmoba, saidanac irkveva, rom sadavo

gaiziara apelantis mosazrebebi imis Sesaxeb, rom igi iyo kooperativ


`fanaskertelis~ mepaie, rom massa da kooperativs Soris arsebobda


raime garigeba da sadavo nagebobis Rirebuleba 8300 lari gaRebul iqna


apelantis mier, vinaidan zemoaRniSnulis damadasturebeli raime


mtkicebuleba saqmeSi ar moipoveba.

redaqciiT) 147-e muxlis Tanaxmad Sps `fanaskerteli~ miiCnia


keTilsindisier myidvelad.

Svilma. kasatorma miuTiTa, rom wlebis manZilze muSaobda Tbilisis


sportkomitetSi frenburTis sportuli bazis direqtoris

aRmoaCnda. kasatoris TqmiT, man ikisra sakuTari saxsrebiT nagebobis

xelSekrulebis mxareebi iyvnen i. n-Svili da t. n-Svili. Sesabamisad,

warmoSoba maSin, roca es gaTvaliswinebulia xelSekrulebiT. amave


kodeqsis 182-e muxlis Sesabamisad solidaruli moTxovnis SemTxvevaSi

da pirveli instanciis sasamarTlom sworad gamoiyena samoqalaqo

n. k-Zem 2000 wlis 3 ivniss d. b-Svilis winaaRmdeg sarCeliT mimarTa


Telavis raionul sasamarTlos.


mosarCelem miuTiTa, rom d. b-Svilma mas ndobis borotad


gamoyenebiT da motyuebiT gamosZala 2250 aSS dolari.


aRniSnuli gamoixata SemdegSi: d. b-Svilma icoda, rom n. k-Zes


esaWiroeboda fuli da asesxa 1500 aSS dolari 15%-is sargebliT. 1999


wlis 30 agvistos, notariusTan gaaformebina sesxis da giravnobis


xelSekruleba 3000 aSS dolarze. giraoSi msesxebels Caadebina 7000 aSS


dolarad Rirebuli aveji, romelic 3000 aSS dolarad Seafasa.


1999 wlis oqtomberSi es aveji xelSekrulebis moTxovnis


sawinaaRmdegod moqalaqe m. l-SvilTan gadaitana da audits


Seafasebina 2000 aSS dolarad.

amisa, mosarCelem moiTxova gonivrul farglebSi moraluri


zianisaTvis fuladi anazRaureba.

wlis 30 agvistos sargeblis gareSe asesxa 3000 aSS dolari. am


xelSekrulebis uzrunvelyofis mizniT man da n. k-Zem urTierTSoris

man gadaitana axloblis e. l-Svilis saxlSi.

gadawyvetilebiT sarCeli ar dakmayofilda.

anazRaurebis moTxovna mosarCelem sasamarTlo proceszeve moxsna.

sasamarTloSi dabruneba Semdegi safuZvliT:


1. kasators miaCnia, rom am saqmeze miRebuli gadawyvetileba kanonis


darRveviTaa gamotanili. misi mosazrebiT, saapelacio sasamarTlom ar


gamoiyena kanoni, romelic unda gamoeyenebina, gamoiyena kanoni, romel-


ic ar unda gamoeyenebina da arasworad ganmarta kanoni. kasators aseve


miaCnia, rom saapelacio sasamarTlos ganCineba dausabuTebelia.

saapelacio saCivari ar Seamowma samarTlebrivi TvalsazrisiT.

sarCelis sagani da safuZveli, riTac daarRvia samoqalaqo saproceso


kodeqsis 248-e muxlis moTxovna.

TviTon sargeblobda.


5. kasatoris mosazrebiT saapelacio sasamarTlom arasworad


miuTiTa, rom man ver warmoadgina saTanado mtkicebulebebi giravno-


bis xelSekrulebis motyuebiT dadebis Sesaxeb.


misi mosazrebiT, sadavo garigeba motyuebiT ki ar daido, aramed


uflebis borotad gamoyenebiT, iZulebiT, rasac xelSekrulebis


Sinaarsic adasturebs. mas miaCnia, rom normalur pirobebSi aseTi


garigeba ar daideboda, radgan dagiravebuli sagnis Rirebuleba


aSkarad Seusabamoa uzrunvelyofis saSualebis RirebulebasTan.


misi mosazrebiT, saapelacio sasamarTlom arasworad ganmarta


samoqalaqo saproceso kodeqsis 102-e muxlis moTxovna, rac imaSi


gamoixata, rom saapelacio sasamarTlom ar gaiziara misi argumentebi,


romlebic kanonis imperatiuli moTxovnidan gamomdinareobda da


daeyrdno falsificirebul mtkicebulebebs. konkretul SemTxvevaSi


avejis n. k-Zis saxlidan gataniT Sewyda ra giravnobis xelSekruleba,


sasamarTlom gauqmebuli giravnobis xelSekrulebaze dayrdnobiT


miiRo ukanono gadawyvetileba.

aseve arasworia kasatoris miTiTeba imis Sesaxeb, rom TiTqos


saapelacio sasamarTlom Segnebulad daarRvia samoqalaqo kodeqsis

bidan gamomdinareobda, msjelobis sagnad ar aqcia da ganCinebidan ar

4 muxlis moTxovnas mainc ver daarRvevda, radgan miTiTebuli muxli


mxareTa SejibrebiTobis principebs aregulirebs da miuTiTebs, rom

mier wamoyenebuli moTxovnebi, mosazrebebi Tu mtkicebulebebi. mxa-


reebi TviTonve gansazRvraven, Tu romeli faqtebi unda daedos


safuZvlad maT moTxovnebs an romeli mtkicebulebiT unda iqnes


dadasturebuli es faqtebi.
